<user_id>108863554728779868578<//user_id><Name>Rosanna Sampson</Name><time>1529794414345<//time><Rating>5< /Rating><review>I have suffered from severe TMJ disfunction for the last 2 years. I tried several dentists, physical therapists and orthodontists before finding Dr. Woodlief. He has been the only one to help my TMJ! I am a young woman in my 30's, and enjoy playing the violin. My TMJ had gotten so bad that my jaw would freeze when I was trying to open my mouth take a bite of food! I would have to put down my spoon, wait a minute, then try to open my mouth again. The pain and pressure in my jaw and forehead got so bad that I had to completely give up playing my violin, which devastated me! By the time I found Dr Woodlief, I could only open my mouth 24mm, which he told me at my first appointment, that a normal mouth should be able to open at least 45-52 mm! No wonder I was in so much pain and discomfort! Dr. Woodlief started my treatment by having me wear a custom made pivot appliance, which fit on my mandible and was so small and unobtrusive, I quickly got used to it, and wore it constantly. Within 1 month, I could start opening my jaw farther, and combined with his prolotherapy injections in my TMJ, within 9 months, I could open my jaw 52mm without any clunking or freezing of the TMJ joint! To say that I am ecstatic is an understatement! I have been given my normal life back, thanks to Dr. Woodlief and his amazing staff!! I now am continuing on with further treatment, proceeding with the DNA appliance for a long term solution, to make sure my TMJ problems never come back. Dr Woodlief educated me that my TMJ disfunction was greatly due to my upper arch being extremely narrow and high and the arch of my teeth was shaped like a mushroom instead of a uniform arch. For a person of my stature, 5' 10" and medium build frame, my upper arch was way too small to support all the pressure and pounds of force my TMJ has to withstand when I eat, and when I play violin. I have been in the DNA appliance treatment now for 6 months, and I can tell the difference with how much better I am able to eat and chew my food. I never could chew before with my molars -my front anterior teeth were angled too straight up and down and stopped my jaw from closing like it should and kept my top and lower molars from making contact, so I couldn't chew my food correctly! It's amazing what you just think is normal in your body until you know differently! I am now looking forward to a fuller smile as my arch is being gently widened every month. Oh, and did I mention that I can play my violin again? I cried tears of joy picking up my violin and playing it again, for you see, it is my great-great-grandfather's violin, and my heritage. God bless you, Dr. Woodlief!< /review>< Pics>

<date>1522424840909<//date><Review>Sure, some of the produce is less than fresh, but Food Fair is a neighborhood fixture in North Vacaville. It's been around for ages. They're open 365 days a year, so if you forget halfway through Thanksgiving that you forgot Aunt Sally's secret ingredient in the stuffing, they're going to be there for you. You can pick up just about any alcohol there, too. One of the better grocery store liquor departments in town.

They do not stop until the entire facility is spotless. Junk King offers affordable pricing and convenience. The nice thing is you pay based on how much of the truck is used, instead of hourly labor, gas or disposal costs (which is good, because our job took much longer than I expected based on the amount of stuff to haul). They did an on-site estimate beforehand, and Jacob and his team were very thorough in cleaning out our garage and asking if we wanted to save any items that may have value.

I would especially recommend Junk King if you anticipate insects or rodents found on the job. These guys weren't afraid of some black widow spiders found in our garage.<//Text>
